BL2
#<{mod_name}>

    # {mod_name} v{mod_version}
    # by Apocalyptech
    # Licensed under Public Domain / CC0 1.0 Universal
    #
    # All sorts of tweaks to loot in general, with the aim of basically making all
    # the loot drops in the game "better".  In the default configuration, there is
    # a very increased chance of blues/purples/etech/legendary items across the
    # board, slightly more Eridium, and far better badass and boss drops.  Also
    # basically all game items will be available as regular world drops, including
    # legendaries, uniques, pearls, seraph, and effervescent items.
    #
    # The specifics of much of the mod, however, including drop quality, can be
    # configured below.  Every section apart from "Base Mod Configuration" is
    # intended to be user-configurable.

        #<Base Mod Configuration>

            # This category is mostly considered stuff you'll be unlikely to toggle on/off
            # individually.  The categories which are intended to be user-settable are all below
            # this one, starting with "Legendary and E-Tech Pool Adjustments" and ending with
            # the boss unique quantities.
            #
            # It's not really a "base" config -- at lot of the "meat" of the mod is in the
            # user-selectable areas, but I was at a loss for a better name for it.

            #<Base Early Game Unlocks><lock>

                # There are problems with early-game loot if we don't unlock at least SOME
                # weapon/gear tiers earlier than the game intends.  We're forcing the game to
                # unlock everything from the beginning as if you're already at level seven.
                # UCP does some of this but skips some of the intermediate levels, which
                # can cause problems for us.  So, we're locking this category so that breakage
                # can't happen.  (One of the more egregious problems is the shotgun not
                # spawning in the Hyperion barge at the end of Windshear Waste, which can
                # block mission progress.  Another solution there would be to just not improve
                # that chest, of course, but we'd still have issues with other early-game
                # drops.)

                set GD_Itempools.Scheduling.Gamestage_02:ConstantAttributeValueResolver_0 ConstantValue 1

                set GD_Itempools.Scheduling.Gamestage_03:ConstantAttributeValueResolver_0 ConstantValue 1

                set GD_Itempools.Scheduling.Gamestage_04:ConstantAttributeValueResolver_0 ConstantValue 1

                set GD_Itempools.Scheduling.Gamestage_05:ConstantAttributeValueResolver_0 ConstantValue 1

                set GD_Itempools.Scheduling.Gamestage_06:ConstantAttributeValueResolver_0 ConstantValue 1

                set GD_Itempools.Scheduling.Gamestage_07:ConstantAttributeValueResolver_0 ConstantValue 1

            #</Base Early Game Unlocks>

            #<UCP Duplicates>

                # This section contains various statements which are duplicates of stuff
                # that's in UCP already.  Mostly these are things which were in the original
                # versions of Better Loot, and were added into UCP when 4.1 was released.
                # There's no problem with having both active -- it just means that a few
                # things will be executed twice.  I'm leaving them in here, though, because
                # they're mostly fixes which should be in the base game itself, and that way
                # people who don't use UCP will still get them.

                #<Badass Enemy Fixes>

                    # Various "Badass" enemies in some DLCs were presumably accidentally set to
                    # pull from the standard enemy drop pool, rather than badass.  This section
                    # fixes those up.  UCP 4.1 added this in as a base feature, but we're
                    # keeping it in here regardless.

                    #<Badass Bedrock Bullymong>

                        level None set GD_Population_PrimalBeast.Balance.PawnBalance_PrimalBeast_BedrockBadass DefaultItemPoolIncludedLists[0] ItemPoolListDefinition'GD_Itempools.ListDefs.BadassEnemyGunsAndGear'

                    #</Badass Bedrock Bullymong>

                    #<Badass Boroks>

                        {mp:badass_borok_Corrosive}

                        {mp:badass_borok_Fire}

                        {mp:badass_borok_Shock}

                        {mp:badass_borok_Slag}

                    #</Badass Boroks>

                    #<Badass Fire Archers>

                        level None set GD_Aster_Pop_Knights.Balance.PawnBalance_Knight_BadassFireArcher DefaultItemPoolIncludedLists[0] ItemPoolListDefinition'GD_Itempools.ListDefs.BadassEnemyGunsAndGear'

                    #</Badass Fire Archers>

                    #<Badass Knights>

                        level None set GD_Aster_Pop_Knights.Balance.PawnBalance_Knight_Badass DefaultItemPoolIncludedLists[0] ItemPoolListDefinition'GD_Itempools.ListDefs.BadassEnemyGunsAndGear'

                    #</Badass Knights>

                    #<Badass Yeti>

                        level Xmas_P set GD_Allium_BadassYeti.Balance.PawnBalance_Allium_BadassYeti DefaultItemPoolIncludedLists[0] ItemPoolListDefinition'GD_Itempools.ListDefs.BadassEnemyGunsAndGear'

                    #</Badass Yeti>

                    #<Undead Badass Psychos>

                        level Pumpkin_Patch_P set GD_Pop_HallowSkeleton.Balance.PawnBalance_BadassUndeadPsycho DefaultItemPoolIncludedLists[0] ItemPoolListDefinition'GD_Itempools.ListDefs.BadassEnemyGunsAndGear'

                    #</Undead Badass Psychos>

                    #<Wattle Gobbler Tributes>

                        # Three tributes from the Wattle Gobler Headhunter Pack don't have
                        # any drops defined, but the rest drop from the badass pool.  Fix that.
                        # This was also fixed in the UCP 4.1 update, but we're going to leave
                        # it in here as well.

                        {mp:wattle_tribute_cynder}

                        {mp:wattle_tribute_strip}

                        {mp:wattle_tribute_flay}

                    #</Wattle Gobbler Tributes>

                #</Badass Enemy Fixes>

                #<Fix Broken Treasure Chest Shield Pools>

                    # Various chests in the game have a possible "Shields" item pool which will
                    # never actually trigger in-game because they include an invalid item in the
                    # pool.  This fixes the pool so that it can be chosen again.  This fix is now
                    # included as part of UCP 4.1, but we're leaving it in here anyway.

                    {mp:euphoria_fix_0}

                    {mp:euphoria_fix_1}

                    {mp:euphoria_fix_2}

                    {mp:euphoria_fix_3}

                    {mp:euphoria_fix_4}

                    {mp:euphoria_fix_5}

                    {mp:euphoria_fix_6}

                #</Fix Broken Treasure Chest Shield Pools>

                #<Make Bosses Use Global Drop Probability Constants>

                    # A few bosses had hardcoded probabilities for their unique drops,
                    # rather than using the game's drop probability constants that basically
                    # everything else in the game uses.  This section fixes that up.  (This
                    # fix was also included in UCP 4.1, but we're keeping it in here too.)

                    #<Badass Creeper>

                        level Caverns_P set GD_Population_Creeper.Balance.PawnBalance_CreeperBadass DefaultItemPoolList[0].PoolProbability
                        (
                            BaseValueConstant=0.000000,
                            BaseValueAttribute=AttributeDefinition'GD_Itempools.DropWeights.DropODDS_BossUniques',
                            InitializationDefinition=None,
                            BaseValueScaleConstant=1.250000
                        )

                    #</Badass Creeper>

                    #<Big Sleep>

                        level Orchid_Caves_P set GD_Orchid_Pop_Sandman.Balance.PawnBalance_Orchid_BigSleep DefaultItemPoolList[1].PoolProbability
                        (
                            BaseValueConstant=0,
                            BaseValueAttribute=AttributeDefinition'GD_Itempools.DropWeights.DropODDS_BossUniqueRares',
                            InitializationDefinition=None,
                            BaseValueScaleConstant=1
                        )

                    #</Big Sleep>

                    #<No-Beard>

                        level Orchid_OasisTown_P set GD_Orchid_Pop_NoBeard.PawnBalance_Orchid_NoBeard DefaultItemPoolList[1].PoolProbability
                        (
                            BaseValueConstant=0,
                            BaseValueAttribute=AttributeDefinition'GD_Itempools.DropWeights.DropODDS_BossUniqueRares',
                            InitializationDefinition=None,
                            BaseValueScaleConstant=1
                        )

                    #</No-Beard>

                    #<Piston>

                        level None set GD_Iris_Population_PistonBoss.Balance.Iris_PawnBalance_PistonBoss DefaultItemPoolList[2].PoolProbability
                        (
                            BaseValueConstant=0,
                            BaseValueAttribute=AttributeDefinition'GD_Itempools.DropWeights.DropODDS_BossUniqueRares',
                            InitializationDefinition=None,
                            BaseValueScaleConstant=1
                        )

                    #</Piston>

                #</Make Bosses Use Global Drop Probability Constants>

            #</UCP Duplicates>

            #<Loot Pool Tweaks>

                # Note that more loot pool tweaks occur inside the "Drop Quality" section
                # down below.

                #<Normalize Gun Type Drops>

                    # In the vanilla game, pistols are the most likely drop, followed by
                    # ARs/SMGs/Shotguns, then snipers, and then launchers.  This normalizes
                    # the probabilities for Pistols/ARs/SMGs/Shotguns, and makes snipers and
                    # launchers more likely (though still not as likely as the others)

                    {mp:normalize_weapon_types_Common_Pistol}

                    {mp:normalize_weapon_types_Uncommon_Pistol}

                    {mp:normalize_weapon_types_Rare_Pistol}

                    {mp:normalize_weapon_types_VeryRare_Pistol}

                    {mp:normalize_weapon_types_VeryRare_Alien_Pistol}

                    {mp:normalize_weapon_types_Legendary_Pistol}

                    {mp:normalize_weapon_types_Common_AR}

                    {mp:normalize_weapon_types_Uncommon_AR}

                    {mp:normalize_weapon_types_Rare_AR}

                    {mp:normalize_weapon_types_VeryRare_AR}

                    {mp:normalize_weapon_types_VeryRare_Alien_AR}

                    {mp:normalize_weapon_types_Legendary_AR}

                    {mp:normalize_weapon_types_Common_SMG}

                    {mp:normalize_weapon_types_Uncommon_SMG}

                    {mp:normalize_weapon_types_Rare_SMG}

                    {mp:normalize_weapon_types_VeryRare_SMG}

                    {mp:normalize_weapon_types_VeryRare_Alien_SMG}

                    {mp:normalize_weapon_types_Legendary_SMG}

                    {mp:normalize_weapon_types_Common_Shotgun}

                    {mp:normalize_weapon_types_Uncommon_Shotgun}

                    {mp:normalize_weapon_types_Rare_Shotgun}

                    {mp:normalize_weapon_types_VeryRare_Shotgun}

                    {mp:normalize_weapon_types_VeryRare_Alien_Shotgun}

                    {mp:normalize_weapon_types_Legendary_Shotgun}

                    {mp:normalize_weapon_types_Common_Sniper}

                    {mp:normalize_weapon_types_Uncommon_Sniper}

                    {mp:normalize_weapon_types_Rare_Sniper}

                    {mp:normalize_weapon_types_VeryRare_Sniper}

                    {mp:normalize_weapon_types_VeryRare_Alien_Sniper}

                    {mp:normalize_weapon_types_Legendary_Sniper}

                    {mp:normalize_weapon_types_Common_Launcher}

                    {mp:normalize_weapon_types_Uncommon_Launcher}

                    {mp:normalize_weapon_types_Rare_Launcher}

                    {mp:normalize_weapon_types_VeryRare_Launcher}

                    {mp:normalize_weapon_types_VeryRare_Alien_Launcher}

                    {mp:normalize_weapon_types_Legendary_Launcher}

                #</Normalize Gun Type Drops>

                #<Equalize Tiny Tina DLC Gemstone Distribution>

                    # The default Gemstone pool in the Tiny Tina DLC vastly weights pistols
                    # over the others.  This sets them all equal.  (I'd noticed this thanks
                    # to Orudeon's "Gemstone Loot Pools")

                    set GD_Aster_ItemPools.WeaponPools.Pool_Weapons_04_Gemstone BalancedItems
                    (
                        (
                            ItmPoolDefinition=ItemPoolDefinition'GD_Aster_ItemPools.WeaponPools.Pool_Weapons_Pistols_04_Gemstone',
                            InvBalanceDefinition=None,
                            Probability=(
                                BaseValueConstant=1.000000,
                                BaseValueAttribute=None,
                                InitializationDefinition=None,
                                BaseValueScaleConstant=1.000000
                            ),
                            bDropOnDeath=True
                        ),
                        (
                            ItmPoolDefinition=ItemPoolDefinition'GD_Aster_ItemPools.WeaponPools.Pool_Weapons_Shotguns_04_Gemstone',
                            InvBalanceDefinition=None,
                            Probability=(
                                BaseValueConstant=1.000000,
                                BaseValueAttribute=None,
                                InitializationDefinition=None,
                                BaseValueScaleConstant=1.000000
                            ),
                            bDropOnDeath=True
                        ),
                        (
                            ItmPoolDefinition=ItemPoolDefinition'GD_Aster_ItemPools.WeaponPools.Pool_Weapons_SMGs_04_Gemstone',
                            InvBalanceDefinition=None,
                            Probability=(
                                BaseValueConstant=1.000000,
                                BaseValueAttribute=None,
                                InitializationDefinition=None,
                                BaseValueScaleConstant=1.000000
                            ),
                            bDropOnDeath=True
                        ),
                        (
                            ItmPoolDefinition=ItemPoolDefinition'GD_Aster_ItemPools.WeaponPools.Pool_Weapons_ARs_04_Gemstone',
                            InvBalanceDefinition=None,
                            Probability=(
                                BaseValueConstant=1.000000,
                                BaseValueAttribute=None,
                                InitializationDefinition=None,
                                BaseValueScaleConstant=1.000000
                            ),
                            bDropOnDeath=True
                        ),
                        (
                            ItmPoolDefinition=ItemPoolDefinition'GD_Aster_ItemPools.WeaponPools.Pool_Weapons_Snipers_04_Gemstone',
                            InvBalanceDefinition=None,
                            Probability=(
                                BaseValueConstant=1.000000,
                                BaseValueAttribute=None,
                                InitializationDefinition=None,
                                BaseValueScaleConstant=1.000000
                            ),
                            bDropOnDeath=True
                        )
                    )

                #</Equalize Tiny Tina DLC Gemstone Distribution>

                #<Force Alignment COMs Blue And Higher>

                    # Forces Dragon Keep Alignment COMs to be at least blue rarity.
                    # COMs in the base game are nicely separated into rarity groups
                    # which manage the Alpha/Beta/Gamma attributes via some fancy
                    # property management, but the Dragon Keep ones are all in one
                    # gigantic group.  So, we alter the main pools to just exclude
                    # the lower-quality parts, like Noskill/AS1/AS2 in Alpha, and
                    # the x0/x1 levels in Beta and Gamma.

                    set GD_Aster_ItemGrades.ClassMods.BalDef_ClassMod_Aster_Assassin:ItemPartListCollectionDefinition_42 AlphaPartData
                    (
                        bEnabled=True,

                #<Nerfed Containers>

                    # Prior to v1.2.0 of this mod, various smaller containers (cardboard boxes,
                    # dumpsters, etc) would have a chance to drop from weapon pools whose
                    # probabilities we didn't alter, so they would generally end up being whites
                    # or greens.  Some changes in v1.2.0 made them start using the enhanced
                    # weights, and I've found I prefer these containers to continue having junk
                    # for loot, actually.  So, these statements will nerf those containers down
                    # to only ever getting common gear.

                #<Better Badass Pool Definitions>

                    # Improvements for a few badass-style enemies.  Note that improvements to
                    # the main Badass pools happen inside the "Drop Quality" section, so check
                    # there as well.

                    #<Chubby Enemies>

                        # Unfortunately, this has to be done via Hotfix.  GD_Itempools.ListDefs.ChubbyEnemyGunsAndGear
                        # is defined in the base files, and can be altered via "set", but Lobelia uses some kind of
                        # hotfix of its own to alter the pool when levels get loaded, which will overwrite various
                        # values in there.  So, we have to put it in as a hotfix at the end, instead.

                        level None set GD_Itempools.ListDefs.ChubbyEnemyGunsAndGear ItemPools
                        (
                            (
                                ItemPool=ItemPoolDefinition'GD_Itempools.Runnables.Pool_ChubbieUniques',
                                PoolProbability=(
                                    BaseValueConstant=1.000000,
                                    BaseValueAttribute=None,
                                    InitializationDefinition=None,
                                    BaseValueScaleConstant=1.000000
                                )
                            ),
                            (
                                ItemPool=ItemPoolDefinition'GD_Itempools.EnemyDropPools.Pool_GunsAndGear_05_VeryRare',
                                PoolProbability=(
                                    BaseValueConstant=1.000000,
                                    BaseValueAttribute=None,
                                    InitializationDefinition=None,
                                    BaseValueScaleConstant=1.000000
                                )
                            ),
                            (
                                ItemPool=ItemPoolDefinition'GD_Itempools.GeneralItemPools.Pool_GunsAndGear',
                                PoolProbability=(
                                    BaseValueConstant=1.000000,
                                    BaseValueAttribute=None,
                                    InitializationDefinition=None,
                                    BaseValueScaleConstant=1.000000
                                )
                            ),
                            (

                #</Boss Drop Normalization>

                #<Raid Boss Drop Improvements>

                    # This improves drops from raid bosses, which IMO are often quite anemic.
                    # They will drop more Eridium, more rare gear, and will drop N
                    # legendaries/uniques/pearls for all possible weapons in that pool.
                    # They will also drop more Seraph crystals, and will drop crystals even
                    # in Normal/TVHM.  Note that the Raid bosses also benefit from various
                    # changes we've made elsewhere in the mod, to the point that a few of
                    # them don't even need any specific tweaking in this section (which is
                    # why Terramorphous, Vermivorous, and Son of Crawmerax don't have a
                    # section in here).

                    #<Voracidous>

                        # We're playing a strange game with the drop pool here.  Unlike
                        # other DLCs, the item definition for the seraph crystals doesn't get
                        # loaded until the level does, so we can't specify seraph crystal
                        # rewards directly.  Rather than have a gigantic hotfix, what I'm doing
                        # is substituting GD_Itempools.WeaponPools.Pool_Weapons_All_01_Common
                        # and then just hotfixing *those* values.
                        #
                        # Additionally, Vorac and Dexi both drop from the same pool.  We'd want to
                        # update the quantity for Vorac's drops, but can't because Dexi's drops
                        # would be insane then (since it drops multiple times).  So the same
                        # unique pools get specified in here multiple times.
                        #
                        # We're using the magic number .42 in the seraph/legendary pools so
                        # that our later quantity hotfixes can apply correctly if this section
                        # is activated, and do nothing if it's not.  Wouldn't want to do weird
                        # things to a pool in an unknown state.

                #<Enemy Drop Nerfs>

                    # A few enemies end up dropping loot a bit too much even for my tastes.
                    # This section nerfs them a bit to be slightly more reasonable.

                    #<Skeleton Kings>

                        # UCP adds the Emperor as a drop for the four Skeleton Kings in the
                        # Dragon Keep DLC.  They drop at a reduced rate already, but we're
                        # going to drop them down a little bit further.

                        level Dead_Forest_P set GD_Aster_Pop_Skeletons.Balance.PawnBalance_SkeletonKing_Aliah DefaultItemPoolList[0].PoolProbability.BaseValueScaleConstant 0.333333

                        level Dead_Forest_P set GD_Aster_Pop_Skeletons.Balance.PawnBalance_SkeletonKing_Crono DefaultItemPoolList[0].PoolProbability.BaseValueScaleConstant 0.333333

                        level Dead_Forest_P set GD_Aster_Pop_Skeletons.Balance.PawnBalance_SkeletonKing_Nazar DefaultItemPoolList[0].PoolProbability.BaseValueScaleConstant 0.333333

                        level Dead_Forest_P set GD_Aster_Pop_Skeletons.Balance.PawnBalance_SkeletonKing_Seth DefaultItemPoolList[0].PoolProbability.BaseValueScaleConstant 0.333333

                    #</Skeleton Kings>

                    #<Treants>

                        # Treants drop the Bee at usual boss-level drop rates, which is a
                        # bit much since you encounter so many of them throughout the
                        # Dragon Keep DLC.  Scaling their drop rate by 33%

                        level None set GD_Aster_Pop_Treant.Balance.PawnBalance_Treant DefaultItemPoolList[0].PoolProbability.BaseValueScaleConstant 0.333333

                    #</Treants>

                #</Enemy Drop Nerfs>

            #</Better Enemy Drops>

    #</Base Mod Configuration>

    #<Remove Level-Based Loot Restrictions (enhancement of UCP 4.2)>

        # In addition to the basic early-game weapon unlocks that UCP provides, this
        # allows Relics, Class Mods, all shield types, all grenade types, and probably
        # just about everything to spawn from the beginning.
        #
        # Copied from BL2 Early Bloomer v1.1.2 by Apocalyptech, though with a few of the
        # unlocks moved into the main mod section.
        #
        # This section is already also included in BL2 Cold Dead Hands, but there's no problem
        # with having it enabled in both.

{early_game_unlocks}

    #</Remove Level-Based Loot Restrictions (enhancement of UCP 4.2)>

    #<Legendary and E-Tech Pool Adjustments>

        # Categories to alter what items are in the global legendary pools.  First,
        # Gemstones can be added to the E-Tech pool, and then a series of optional
        # categories which can add uniques, pearls, and seraphs into the main legendary
        # pools.  (This does omit a few items such as Captain Blade's Midnight Star, and
        # the Contraband Sky Rocket.)

        #<Base Setup for Pools (don't uncheck this if you choose anything below here)><lock>

            # Various statements to prep our Legendary pools.  Ensures that all of the
            # "standard" legendary items are always in the legendary pool, and leaves
            # room in the pools so that uniques, seraphs, and pearls can be added in later
            # if desired.  Also ensures that the "gladiolus" pools point to our main
            # pools.

            #<Redirect Gladiolus Pools to Main Pools>

                # First up, Gladiolus specifies its own weapon pools, GD_Gladioulus_Itempools.WeaponPools.Pool_Weapons_*_LegendaryPlusPearl,
                # and we want to make sure that anything looking for legendaries looks in our overridden classes here.  So
                # we're going to point all of its custom objects back to the "main" ones which we'll then override

                set GD_Gladiolus_Itempools.WeaponPools.Pool_Weapons_AssaultRifles_07_LegendaryPlusPearl BalancedItems
                (
                    (
                        ItmPoolDefinition=ItemPoolDefinition'GD_Itempools.WeaponPools.Pool_Weapons_AssaultRifles_06_Legendary',
                        InvBalanceDefinition=None,
                        Probability=(
                            BaseValueConstant=1.000000,
                            BaseValueAttribute=None,
                            InitializationDefinition=None,
                            BaseValueScaleConstant=1.000000
                        ),
                        bDropOnDeath=True
                    )
                )

                set GD_Gladiolus_Itempools.WeaponPools.Pool_Weapons_Launchers_07_LegendaryPlusPearl BalancedItems
                (
                    (
                        ItmPoolDefinition=ItemPoolDefinition'GD_Itempools.WeaponPools.Pool_Weapons_Launchers_06_Legendary',

            #<Relic Pool Setup>

                # Note that the Relic pools work totally differently than every other
                # item's pools.  There ARE some rarity-level pools, but relics don't
                # actually work that way, and basically nothing uses them.  So what we do
                # is play some games with weights and just add in legendaries, etc, to the
                # "Reward" relic pool.  This means that Relics get their own custom
                # weights in our code, which won't actually match everything else exactly.

                            BaseValueScaleConstant=0
                        ),
                        bDropOnDeath=True
                    )
                )

                set GD_Itempools.ArtifactPools.Pool_Artifacts_05_Legendary BalancedItems
                (
                    (
                        ItmPoolDefinition=ItemPoolDefinition'GD_Itempools.ArtifactPools.Pool_ArtifactsReward',
                        InvBalanceDefinition=None,
                        Probability=(
                            BaseValueConstant=1.000000,
                            BaseValueAttribute=None,
                            InitializationDefinition=None,
                            BaseValueScaleConstant=1.000000
                        ),
                        bDropOnDeath=True
                    )
                )

            #</Relic Pool Setup>

            # some nice boosts).
